Features
Ports & Slots
Reviews
PURESIGHT PRO
Precision in Every Pixel
Precise visuals pop on a 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with perfect color accuracy, 120Hz refresh rate, and HDR brilliance. A 90.8% screen-to-body ratio expands your view, while TÜV low blue light tech reduces eye strain for marathon sessions.
MORE PRODUCTIVE AND CREATIVE
It's Possible on Your Intel® AI PC
Work, create, innovate, and experience the best AI PC performance with Intel® Core™ Ultra processors. AI acceleration via a 72 TOPS iGPU optimizes workflows, speeding up creative tasks like animation, 3D rendering, and video editing. The ultimate performance lets you do more with ease, without sacrificing peace of mind. 
LENOVO X POWER
Create at the Speed of X
The overclocked RAM helps push performance to new levels, valuable for high-bandwidth tasks like video editing or data processing. AIDA64 memory benchmark testing shows significant improvements, including faster data transfer and reduced latency.
WELCOME TO LENOVO AURA EDITION
Signature Imagination with Intel®
Lenovo and Intel® have long joined forces to engineer the best laptops in the industry. Our years of deep collaboration now culminate in bold new software solutions that elevate your day-to-day experience. The best products. The best experiences. Lenovo Aura Edition.
MULTIDEVICE SYNC
Just Tap to Connect
Smart Share connects your smartphone to your laptop instantly via an AI virtual sensor. Just tap your Android™ or iOS device on your laptop — then drag and drop. Edit photos and share easily. Plus, access and send text messages from your PC.*

*To use the tap-and-share feature, the Smart Share app must be running.
EXPERIENCE THE INTELLIGENCE OF AURA
Smart Modes, Smarter Technology
*Selected models may require a software update to access all features shown in the images and videos.
Collaboration Mode
Improve your virtual meeting experiences. Keep the focus on you with background blur, low-light enhancer, autoframing, and a virtual presenter. Preview video before joining a call. Expect more engaging communication that puts you in control.
Attention Mode
Minimize distractions so you can focus. You choose the domains and apps you want to block for a set amount of time to keep you immersed in the task at hand.
Power Mode
Reduce power consumption and boost performance when unplugged. Power Mode optimizes settings and finds the ideal balance between improved battery life and better battery performance.
Wellness Mode
Promote digital well-being to keep your health at the forefront. Alerts encourage breaks for your eyes, with clear guidance to shift your sight to something in the distance. Plus, relying on Al sensors, reminders foster good ergonomic habits.
Shield Mode
Proactively enhance data security and privacy. This mode prompts for your preferred VPN when connecting to WiFi, notifies you if someone looks over your shoulder, and blurs your screen to guard privacy if someone is detected near your device.
TECH SUPPORT 24/7
No IT? No Problem!
With Smart Care, you’ll enjoy convenient and quick access to tech expertise! No need to find a store — we provide options to connect to our geniuses virtually, so you stay up and running.*

*Limited global availability. To unlock all features described above requires a valid Lenovo Support agreement (additional charges may apply).
PURESIGHT PRO WITH TOUCHSCREEN
Bring Your Vision to Life
Bring your creativity to life on the 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with 100% P3 and Adobe RGB color gamut. Experience true-to-life colors, smooth 120Hz motion, 1000nit peak brightness, and HDR brilliance. Enjoy expansive views while TÜV-certified low blue light reduces eye strain, keeping you comfortable during long creative sessions.
PURESIGHT PRO
Visuals, Perfected
See Every Detail Unfold
Catch perfect details on a DisplayHDR True Black 1000-certified OLED display with HDR 1000 nits’ peak brightness. Enjoy vibrant colors, lifelike accuracy, and enhanced highlights and shadow details. Create, edit, and watch HDR content with clarity.
See Your World in True Color
Score professional color gamut with 100% Adobe RGB and P3, plus Delta E<1 color accuracy. Enjoy 10-bit color depth and precise reproduction for detailed edits, vivid visuals, and cinema-quality content. Keep your work true to your vision.
Every Frame, Fluid and Clear
A 120Hz refresh rate delivers sharper frames and fluid transitions. Whether creating animations or watching movies, the smoother motion ensures precise detail, helping content creators achieve professional results with ease.
Focus Longer, Create Better
Create longer and more comfortably with TÜV Low Blue Light, TÜV Eyesafe, and TÜV Flicker-Free certification. Minimize eye strain and fatigue, helping you stay focused during extended sessions, whether you’re creating or multitasking.
PREMIUM SUITE
Work Smarter, Achieve More
The Yoga Keyboard is developed with dynamic force design and Yoga coating to keep you in flow. The silent touchpad glides effortlessly, and Dolby Atmos® sound with four speakers that achieve 80.5db volume and 126Hz low-frequency bass, providing immersive sound. Enjoy clear visuals and noise-canceling mics for every call and project.
The Bliss is in the Details
Precision in Every Keystroke
The Yoga-coated keyboard resists oil and water for a clean, premium feel, while 1.5mm key travel, 0.3mm dish caps, and dynamic force feedback deliver satisfying responsiveness. Designed for comfort, control, and productivity, it’s built to keep up.
Navigate with Effortless Precision
Get precise, quiet navigation with a durable touchpad built to last. Whisper-quiet with every swipe and tap, it’s designed for comfort and control, making it ideal for extended work sessions or creative projects without unnecessary distractions.
Hear More and Feel More
Feel every beat, word, and note over four powerful speakers, certified by Dolby Atmos®. Whether you’re streaming or jamming, the upgraded woofer yields clarity and stunning bass sound that bring each moment to life in incredible depth and detail.
Clear Voice, Crisp Vision
Capture each word clearly with four noise-canceling 3D array mics and 360° spatial audio that picks up voices from all directions. Built-in Voice ID isolates your voice while the 5M IR camera delivers detailed visuals for a professional experience.
LENOVO AI APPS
Smarter, Faster, and Safer
Get more done with Lenovo's AI-powered apps, designed to adapt to your needs. These apps go beyond just simplifying tasks — they personalize your experience, boost productivity, and protect your data. Whether it’s big projects or everyday tasks, Lenovo AI Apps deliver evolving performance with limitless potential to create and achieve more.
YOUR CREATIVE TOOLKIT
Professional Creative Tools, on Us
Your laptop includes a free 2-month membership to Adobe Creative Cloud*. Start a new membership of the entire suite with no payment or credit card information required at time of redemption. Already a member? No problem. Your existing payment method will be paused for two months. (Over $100 added value with no cost to you.) Terms apply. Click here for details!

*Available via Lenovo Vantage
YOGA ACCESSORIES
Seamless Sound and Control
Complete your setup with Yoga Pro 7i Aura Edition’s optional connected gear. The Yoga 14(35.56 cms) Sleeve keeps your PC protected, while the Lenovo TWS Earbuds Yoga PC Edition deliver crystal-clear sound and Active Noise Cancellation (ANC) for immersive audio. The Pro Mouse provides smooth, wireless navigation for your everyday use.

*Wireless mouse and earbuds shown with laptop sold separately.
A PC BUILT RESPONSIBLY
Sustainability
A step towards a finer planet, the Carbon Neutral Certified*, ENERGY STAR®-rated, and EPEAT® Gold-registered** Yoga Pro 7i Aura Edition achieves plastic-free packaging. All paper boxes used in packaging are FSC™-certified and made from other controlled material.*** It's built with 50% recycled aluminum in the bottom cover. 

*Based on reduction efforts and carbon offset purchases. Learn more about the carbon-neutral reports at https://www.lenovo.com/in/en/carbonneutral. Carbon neutrality certification was issued by TÜV Rheinland Greater China in accordance with PAS 2060:2014 Specification for the Demonstration of Carbon Neutrality. Learn more about our carbon-neutral reports at https://www.lenovo.com/in/en/carbonneutral
**EPEAT-registered where applicable -- see www.epeat.net for registration status by country.

Extremely Disappointed – Bluetooth Mic Doesnt Work
Kothuru Manoj Kumar
VERIFIED PURCHASER
5 months ago
Bought the Lenovo Yoga 7i Aura Edition expecting a premium device, but it fails at the basics. The Bluetooth headset mic doesn’t work in any apps — only in Windows test mode. It’s like buying a luxury car that can’t honk. Disabling Dolby Atmos temporarily fixes it, proving it’s a software flaw. Lenovo support couldn’t resolve it even after sending a technician. Not recommended until they fix this issue.

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now

4 out of 5 stars.
A Everyday Laptop with Premium Build and Display
Akash_K
VERIFIED PURCHASER
8 months ago
The laptop is overall very good. Its standout feature is the display — sharp, bright, and excellent in quality, though it tends to pick up fingerprints easily. The touchscreen works smoothly, and the keyboard is one of the best I’ve used so far. The trackpad, however, could have been better. In terms of performance, it handles my everyday tasks well, including heavy browser use, AI tools, and Microsoft Office. The battery backup is decent — not exceptional but reliable enough for regular work. The charger adapter gets slightly warm during use, but nothing concerning. The body material feels premium, being fully metal, yet it is light and very easy to carry.

OUR PROMISE TO YOU
Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.

PURESIGHT PRO
Precision in Every Pixel
Precise visuals pop on a 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with perfect color accuracy, 120Hz refresh rate, and HDR brilliance. A 90.8% screen-to-body ratio expands your view, while TÜV low blue light tech reduces eye strain for marathon sessions.
MORE PRODUCTIVE AND CREATIVE
It's Possible on Your Intel® AI PC
Work, create, innovate, and experience the best AI PC performance with Intel® Core™ Ultra processors. AI acceleration via a 72 TOPS iGPU optimizes workflows, speeding up creative tasks like animation, 3D rendering, and video editing. The ultimate performance lets you do more with ease, without sacrificing peace of mind. 
LENOVO X POWER
Create at the Speed of X
The overclocked RAM helps push performance to new levels, valuable for high-bandwidth tasks like video editing or data processing. AIDA64 memory benchmark testing shows significant improvements, including faster data transfer and reduced latency.
WELCOME TO LENOVO AURA EDITION
Signature Imagination with Intel®
Lenovo and Intel® have long joined forces to engineer the best laptops in the industry. Our years of deep collaboration now culminate in bold new software solutions that elevate your day-to-day experience. The best products. The best experiences. Lenovo Aura Edition.
MULTIDEVICE SYNC
Just Tap to Connect
Smart Share connects your smartphone to your laptop instantly via an AI virtual sensor. Just tap your Android™ or iOS device on your laptop — then drag and drop. Edit photos and share easily. Plus, access and send text messages from your PC.*

*To use the tap-and-share feature, the Smart Share app must be running.
EXPERIENCE THE INTELLIGENCE OF AURA
Smart Modes, Smarter Technology
*Selected models may require a software update to access all features shown in the images and videos.
Collaboration Mode
Improve your virtual meeting experiences. Keep the focus on you with background blur, low-light enhancer, autoframing, and a virtual presenter. Preview video before joining a call. Expect more engaging communication that puts you in control.
Attention Mode
Minimize distractions so you can focus. You choose the domains and apps you want to block for a set amount of time to keep you immersed in the task at hand.
Power Mode
Reduce power consumption and boost performance when unplugged. Power Mode optimizes settings and finds the ideal balance between improved battery life and better battery performance.
Wellness Mode
Promote digital well-being to keep your health at the forefront. Alerts encourage breaks for your eyes, with clear guidance to shift your sight to something in the distance. Plus, relying on Al sensors, reminders foster good ergonomic habits.
Shield Mode
Proactively enhance data security and privacy. This mode prompts for your preferred VPN when connecting to WiFi, notifies you if someone looks over your shoulder, and blurs your screen to guard privacy if someone is detected near your device.
TECH SUPPORT 24/7
No IT? No Problem!
With Smart Care, you’ll enjoy convenient and quick access to tech expertise! No need to find a store — we provide options to connect to our geniuses virtually, so you stay up and running.*

*Limited global availability. To unlock all features described above requires a valid Lenovo Support agreement (additional charges may apply).
PURESIGHT PRO WITH TOUCHSCREEN
Bring Your Vision to Life
Bring your creativity to life on the 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with 100% P3 and Adobe RGB color gamut. Experience true-to-life colors, smooth 120Hz motion, 1000nit peak brightness, and HDR brilliance. Enjoy expansive views while TÜV-certified low blue light reduces eye strain, keeping you comfortable during long creative sessions.
PURESIGHT PRO
Visuals, Perfected
See Every Detail Unfold
Catch perfect details on a DisplayHDR True Black 1000-certified OLED display with HDR 1000 nits’ peak brightness. Enjoy vibrant colors, lifelike accuracy, and enhanced highlights and shadow details. Create, edit, and watch HDR content with clarity.
See Your World in True Color
Score professional color gamut with 100% Adobe RGB and P3, plus Delta E<1 color accuracy. Enjoy 10-bit color depth and precise reproduction for detailed edits, vivid visuals, and cinema-quality content. Keep your work true to your vision.
Every Frame, Fluid and Clear
A 120Hz refresh rate delivers sharper frames and fluid transitions. Whether creating animations or watching movies, the smoother motion ensures precise detail, helping content creators achieve professional results with ease.
Focus Longer, Create Better
Create longer and more comfortably with TÜV Low Blue Light, TÜV Eyesafe, and TÜV Flicker-Free certification. Minimize eye strain and fatigue, helping you stay focused during extended sessions, whether you’re creating or multitasking.
PREMIUM SUITE
Work Smarter, Achieve More
The Yoga Keyboard is developed with dynamic force design and Yoga coating to keep you in flow. The silent touchpad glides effortlessly, and Dolby Atmos® sound with four speakers that achieve 80.5db volume and 126Hz low-frequency bass, providing immersive sound. Enjoy clear visuals and noise-canceling mics for every call and project.
The Bliss is in the Details
Precision in Every Keystroke
The Yoga-coated keyboard resists oil and water for a clean, premium feel, while 1.5mm key travel, 0.3mm dish caps, and dynamic force feedback deliver satisfying responsiveness. Designed for comfort, control, and productivity, it’s built to keep up.
Navigate with Effortless Precision
Get precise, quiet navigation with a durable touchpad built to last. Whisper-quiet with every swipe and tap, it’s designed for comfort and control, making it ideal for extended work sessions or creative projects without unnecessary distractions.
Hear More and Feel More
Feel every beat, word, and note over four powerful speakers, certified by Dolby Atmos®. Whether you’re streaming or jamming, the upgraded woofer yields clarity and stunning bass sound that bring each moment to life in incredible depth and detail.
Clear Voice, Crisp Vision
Capture each word clearly with four noise-canceling 3D array mics and 360° spatial audio that picks up voices from all directions. Built-in Voice ID isolates your voice while the 5M IR camera delivers detailed visuals for a professional experience.
LENOVO AI APPS
Smarter, Faster, and Safer
Get more done with Lenovo's AI-powered apps, designed to adapt to your needs. These apps go beyond just simplifying tasks — they personalize your experience, boost productivity, and protect your data. Whether it’s big projects or everyday tasks, Lenovo AI Apps deliver evolving performance with limitless potential to create and achieve more.

Extremely Disappointed – Bluetooth Mic Doesnt Work
Kothuru Manoj Kumar
VERIFIED PURCHASER
5 months ago
Bought the Lenovo Yoga 7i Aura Edition expecting a premium device, but it fails at the basics. The Bluetooth headset mic doesn’t work in any apps — only in Windows test mode. It’s like buying a luxury car that can’t honk. Disabling Dolby Atmos temporarily fixes it, proving it’s a software flaw. Lenovo support couldn’t resolve it even after sending a technician. Not recommended until they fix this issue.

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now

4 out of 5 stars.
A Everyday Laptop with Premium Build and Display
Akash_K
VERIFIED PURCHASER
8 months ago
The laptop is overall very good. Its standout feature is the display — sharp, bright, and excellent in quality, though it tends to pick up fingerprints easily. The touchscreen works smoothly, and the keyboard is one of the best I’ve used so far. The trackpad, however, could have been better. In terms of performance, it handles my everyday tasks well, including heavy browser use, AI tools, and Microsoft Office. The battery backup is decent — not exceptional but reliable enough for regular work. The charger adapter gets slightly warm during use, but nothing concerning. The body material feels premium, being fully metal, yet it is light and very easy to carry.

OUR PROMISE TO YOU
Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.
Learn More >

Precise visuals pop on a 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with perfect color accuracy, 120Hz refresh rate, and HDR brilliance. A 90.8% screen-to-body ratio expands your view, while TÜV low blue light tech reduces eye strain for marathon sessions.
MORE PRODUCTIVE AND CREATIVE
It's Possible on Your Intel® AI PC
Work, create, innovate, and experience the best AI PC performance with Intel® Core™ Ultra processors. AI acceleration via a 72 TOPS iGPU optimizes workflows, speeding up creative tasks like animation, 3D rendering, and video editing. The ultimate performance lets you do more with ease, without sacrificing peace of mind. 
LENOVO X POWER
Create at the Speed of X
The overclocked RAM helps push performance to new levels, valuable for high-bandwidth tasks like video editing or data processing. AIDA64 memory benchmark testing shows significant improvements, including faster data transfer and reduced latency.

Signature Imagination with Intel®
Lenovo and Intel® have long joined forces to engineer the best laptops in the industry. Our years of deep collaboration now culminate in bold new software solutions that elevate your day-to-day experience. The best products. The best experiences. Lenovo Aura Edition.
MULTIDEVICE SYNC
Just Tap to Connect
Smart Share connects your smartphone to your laptop instantly via an AI virtual sensor. Just tap your Android™ or iOS device on your laptop — then drag and drop. Edit photos and share easily. Plus, access and send text messages from your PC.*

*To use the tap-and-share feature, the Smart Share app must be running.
EXPERIENCE THE INTELLIGENCE OF AURA
Smart Modes, Smarter Technology
*Selected models may require a software update to access all features shown in the images and videos.
Collaboration Mode
Improve your virtual meeting experiences. Keep the focus on you with background blur, low-light enhancer, autoframing, and a virtual presenter. Preview video before joining a call. Expect more engaging communication that puts you in control.
Attention Mode
Minimize distractions so you can focus. You choose the domains and apps you want to block for a set amount of time to keep you immersed in the task at hand.
Power Mode
Reduce power consumption and boost performance when unplugged. Power Mode optimizes settings and finds the ideal balance between improved battery life and better battery performance.
Wellness Mode
Promote digital well-being to keep your health at the forefront. Alerts encourage breaks for your eyes, with clear guidance to shift your sight to something in the distance. Plus, relying on Al sensors, reminders foster good ergonomic habits.
Shield Mode
Proactively enhance data security and privacy. This mode prompts for your preferred VPN when connecting to WiFi, notifies you if someone looks over your shoulder, and blurs your screen to guard privacy if someone is detected near your device.

Precision in Every Keystroke
The Yoga-coated keyboard resists oil and water for a clean, premium feel, while 1.5mm key travel, 0.3mm dish caps, and dynamic force feedback deliver satisfying responsiveness. Designed for comfort, control, and productivity, it’s built to keep up.
Navigate with Effortless Precision
Get precise, quiet navigation with a durable touchpad built to last. Whisper-quiet with every swipe and tap, it’s designed for comfort and control, making it ideal for extended work sessions or creative projects without unnecessary distractions.
Hear More and Feel More
Feel every beat, word, and note over four powerful speakers, certified by Dolby Atmos®. Whether you’re streaming or jamming, the upgraded woofer yields clarity and stunning bass sound that bring each moment to life in incredible depth and detail.
Clear Voice, Crisp Vision
Capture each word clearly with four noise-canceling 3D array mics and 360° spatial audio that picks up voices from all directions. Built-in Voice ID isolates your voice while the 5M IR camera delivers detailed visuals for a professional experience.

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now

4 out of 5 stars.
A Everyday Laptop with Premium Build and Display
Akash_K
VERIFIED PURCHASER
8 months ago
The laptop is overall very good. Its standout feature is the display — sharp, bright, and excellent in quality, though it tends to pick up fingerprints easily. The touchscreen works smoothly, and the keyboard is one of the best I’ve used so far. The trackpad, however, could have been better. In terms of performance, it handles my everyday tasks well, including heavy browser use, AI tools, and Microsoft Office. The battery backup is decent — not exceptional but reliable enough for regular work. The charger adapter gets slightly warm during use, but nothing concerning. The body material feels premium, being fully metal, yet it is light and very easy to carry.

OUR PROMISE TO YOU
Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.

Just Tap to Connect

EXPERIENCE THE INTELLIGENCE OF AURA
Smart Modes, Smarter Technology
*Selected models may require a software update to access all features shown in the images and videos.
Collaboration Mode
Improve your virtual meeting experiences. Keep the focus on you with background blur, low-light enhancer, autoframing, and a virtual presenter. Preview video before joining a call. Expect more engaging communication that puts you in control.
Attention Mode
Minimize distractions so you can focus. You choose the domains and apps you want to block for a set amount of time to keep you immersed in the task at hand.
Power Mode
Reduce power consumption and boost performance when unplugged. Power Mode optimizes settings and finds the ideal balance between improved battery life and better battery performance.
Wellness Mode
Promote digital well-being to keep your health at the forefront. Alerts encourage breaks for your eyes, with clear guidance to shift your sight to something in the distance. Plus, relying on Al sensors, reminders foster good ergonomic habits.
Shield Mode
Proactively enhance data security and privacy. This mode prompts for your preferred VPN when connecting to WiFi, notifies you if someone looks over your shoulder, and blurs your screen to guard privacy if someone is detected near your device.

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now

A Everyday Laptop with Premium Build and Display
Akash_K
VERIFIED PURCHASER
8 months ago
The laptop is overall very good. Its standout feature is the display — sharp, bright, and excellent in quality, though it tends to pick up fingerprints easily. The touchscreen works smoothly, and the keyboard is one of the best I’ve used so far. The trackpad, however, could have been better. In terms of performance, it handles my everyday tasks well, including heavy browser use, AI tools, and Microsoft Office. The battery backup is decent — not exceptional but reliable enough for regular work. The charger adapter gets slightly warm during use, but nothing concerning. The body material feels premium, being fully metal, yet it is light and very easy to carry.

OUR PROMISE TO YOU
Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.

Bring Your Vision to Life
Bring your creativity to life on the 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with 100% P3 and Adobe RGB color gamut. Experience true-to-life colors, smooth 120Hz motion, 1000nit peak brightness, and HDR brilliance. Enjoy expansive views while TÜV-certified low blue light reduces eye strain, keeping you comfortable during long creative sessions.
PURESIGHT PRO
Visuals, Perfected
See Every Detail Unfold
Catch perfect details on a DisplayHDR True Black 1000-certified OLED display with HDR 1000 nits’ peak brightness. Enjoy vibrant colors, lifelike accuracy, and enhanced highlights and shadow details. Create, edit, and watch HDR content with clarity.
See Your World in True Color
Score professional color gamut with 100% Adobe RGB and P3, plus Delta E<1 color accuracy. Enjoy 10-bit color depth and precise reproduction for detailed edits, vivid visuals, and cinema-quality content. Keep your work true to your vision.
Every Frame, Fluid and Clear
A 120Hz refresh rate delivers sharper frames and fluid transitions. Whether creating animations or watching movies, the smoother motion ensures precise detail, helping content creators achieve professional results with ease.
Focus Longer, Create Better
Create longer and more comfortably with TÜV Low Blue Light, TÜV Eyesafe, and TÜV Flicker-Free certification. Minimize eye strain and fatigue, helping you stay focused during extended sessions, whether you’re creating or multitasking.
PREMIUM SUITE
Work Smarter, Achieve More
The Yoga Keyboard is developed with dynamic force design and Yoga coating to keep you in flow. The silent touchpad glides effortlessly, and Dolby Atmos® sound with four speakers that achieve 80.5db volume and 126Hz low-frequency bass, providing immersive sound. Enjoy clear visuals and noise-canceling mics for every call and project.
The Bliss is in the Details
Precision in Every Keystroke
The Yoga-coated keyboard resists oil and water for a clean, premium feel, while 1.5mm key travel, 0.3mm dish caps, and dynamic force feedback deliver satisfying responsiveness. Designed for comfort, control, and productivity, it’s built to keep up.
Navigate with Effortless Precision
Get precise, quiet navigation with a durable touchpad built to last. Whisper-quiet with every swipe and tap, it’s designed for comfort and control, making it ideal for extended work sessions or creative projects without unnecessary distractions.
Hear More and Feel More
Feel every beat, word, and note over four powerful speakers, certified by Dolby Atmos®. Whether you’re streaming or jamming, the upgraded woofer yields clarity and stunning bass sound that bring each moment to life in incredible depth and detail.
Clear Voice, Crisp Vision
Capture each word clearly with four noise-canceling 3D array mics and 360° spatial audio that picks up voices from all directions. Built-in Voice ID isolates your voice while the 5M IR camera delivers detailed visuals for a professional experience.
LENOVO AI APPS
Smarter, Faster, and Safer
Get more done with Lenovo's AI-powered apps, designed to adapt to your needs. These apps go beyond just simplifying tasks — they personalize your experience, boost productivity, and protect your data. Whether it’s big projects or everyday tasks, Lenovo AI Apps deliver evolving performance with limitless potential to create and achieve more.
YOUR CREATIVE TOOLKIT
Professional Creative Tools, on Us
Your laptop includes a free 2-month membership to Adobe Creative Cloud*. Start a new membership of the entire suite with no payment or credit card information required at time of redemption. Already a member? No problem. Your existing payment method will be paused for two months. (Over $100 added value with no cost to you.) Terms apply. Click here for details!

*Available via Lenovo Vantage
YOGA ACCESSORIES
Seamless Sound and Control
Complete your setup with Yoga Pro 7i Aura Edition’s optional connected gear. The Yoga 14(35.56 cms) Sleeve keeps your PC protected, while the Lenovo TWS Earbuds Yoga PC Edition deliver crystal-clear sound and Active Noise Cancellation (ANC) for immersive audio. The Pro Mouse provides smooth, wireless navigation for your everyday use.

*Wireless mouse and earbuds shown with laptop sold separately.
A PC BUILT RESPONSIBLY
Sustainability
A step towards a finer planet, the Carbon Neutral Certified*, ENERGY STAR®-rated, and EPEAT® Gold-registered** Yoga Pro 7i Aura Edition achieves plastic-free packaging. All paper boxes used in packaging are FSC™-certified and made from other controlled material.*** It's built with 50% recycled aluminum in the bottom cover.

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now

A Everyday Laptop with Premium Build and Display
Akash_K
VERIFIED PURCHASER
8 months ago
The laptop is overall very good. Its standout feature is the display — sharp, bright, and excellent in quality, though it tends to pick up fingerprints easily. The touchscreen works smoothly, and the keyboard is one of the best I’ve used so far. The trackpad, however, could have been better. In terms of performance, it handles my everyday tasks well, including heavy browser use, AI tools, and Microsoft Office. The battery backup is decent — not exceptional but reliable enough for regular work. The charger adapter gets slightly warm during use, but nothing concerning. The body material feels premium, being fully metal, yet it is light and very easy to carry.

OUR PROMISE TO YOU
Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.

Features
Ports & Slots
Reviews
PURESIGHT PRO
Precision in Every Pixel
Precise visuals pop on a 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with perfect color accuracy, 120Hz refresh rate, and HDR brilliance. A 90.8% screen-to-body ratio expands your view, while TÜV low blue light tech reduces eye strain for marathon sessions.
MORE PRODUCTIVE AND CREATIVE
It's Possible on Your Intel® AI PC
Work, create, innovate, and experience the best AI PC performance with Intel® Core™ Ultra processors. AI acceleration via a 72 TOPS iGPU optimizes workflows, speeding up creative tasks like animation, 3D rendering, and video editing. The ultimate performance lets you do more with ease, without sacrificing peace of mind. 
LENOVO X POWER
Create at the Speed of X
The overclocked RAM helps push performance to new levels, valuable for high-bandwidth tasks like video editing or data processing. AIDA64 memory benchmark testing shows significant improvements, including faster data transfer and reduced latency.
WELCOME TO LENOVO AURA EDITION
Signature Imagination with Intel®
Lenovo and Intel® have long joined forces to engineer the best laptops in the industry. Our years of deep collaboration now culminate in bold new software solutions that elevate your day-to-day experience. The best products. The best experiences. Lenovo Aura Edition.
MULTIDEVICE SYNC
Just Tap to Connect
Smart Share connects your smartphone to your laptop instantly via an AI virtual sensor. Just tap your Android™ or iOS device on your laptop — then drag and drop. Edit photos and share easily. Plus, access and send text messages from your PC.*

*To use the tap-and-share feature, the Smart Share app must be running.
EXPERIENCE THE INTELLIGENCE OF AURA
Smart Modes, Smarter Technology
*Selected models may require a software update to access all features shown in the images and videos.
Collaboration Mode
Improve your virtual meeting experiences. Keep the focus on you with background blur, low-light enhancer, autoframing, and a virtual presenter. Preview video before joining a call. Expect more engaging communication that puts you in control.
Attention Mode
Minimize distractions so you can focus. You choose the domains and apps you want to block for a set amount of time to keep you immersed in the task at hand.
Power Mode
Reduce power consumption and boost performance when unplugged. Power Mode optimizes settings and finds the ideal balance between improved battery life and better battery performance.
Wellness Mode
Promote digital well-being to keep your health at the forefront. Alerts encourage breaks for your eyes, with clear guidance to shift your sight to something in the distance. Plus, relying on Al sensors, reminders foster good ergonomic habits.
Shield Mode
Proactively enhance data security and privacy. This mode prompts for your preferred VPN when connecting to WiFi, notifies you if someone looks over your shoulder, and blurs your screen to guard privacy if someone is detected near your device.
TECH SUPPORT 24/7
No IT? No Problem!
With Smart Care, you’ll enjoy convenient and quick access to tech expertise! No need to find a store — we provide options to connect to our geniuses virtually, so you stay up and running.*

*Limited global availability. To unlock all features described above requires a valid Lenovo Support agreement (additional charges may apply).
PURESIGHT PRO WITH TOUCHSCREEN
Bring Your Vision to Life
Bring your creativity to life on the 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with 100% P3 and Adobe RGB color gamut. Experience true-to-life colors, smooth 120Hz motion, 1000nit peak brightness, and HDR brilliance. Enjoy expansive views while TÜV-certified low blue light reduces eye strain, keeping you comfortable during long creative sessions.
PURESIGHT PRO
Visuals, Perfected
See Every Detail Unfold
Catch perfect details on a DisplayHDR True Black 1000-certified OLED display with HDR 1000 nits’ peak brightness. Enjoy vibrant colors, lifelike accuracy, and enhanced highlights and shadow details. Create, edit, and watch HDR content with clarity.
See Your World in True Color
Score professional color gamut with 100% Adobe RGB and P3, plus Delta E<1 color accuracy. Enjoy 10-bit color depth and precise reproduction for detailed edits, vivid visuals, and cinema-quality content. Keep your work true to your vision.
Every Frame, Fluid and Clear
A 120Hz refresh rate delivers sharper frames and fluid transitions. Whether creating animations or watching movies, the smoother motion ensures precise detail, helping content creators achieve professional results with ease.
Focus Longer, Create Better
Create longer and more comfortably with TÜV Low Blue Light, TÜV Eyesafe, and TÜV Flicker-Free certification. Minimize eye strain and fatigue, helping you stay focused during extended sessions, whether you’re creating or multitasking.
PREMIUM SUITE
Work Smarter, Achieve More
The Yoga Keyboard is developed with dynamic force design and Yoga coating to keep you in flow. The silent touchpad glides effortlessly, and Dolby Atmos® sound with four speakers that achieve 80.5db volume and 126Hz low-frequency bass, providing immersive sound. Enjoy clear visuals and noise-canceling mics for every call and project.
The Bliss is in the Details
Precision in Every Keystroke
The Yoga-coated keyboard resists oil and water for a clean, premium feel, while 1.5mm key travel, 0.3mm dish caps, and dynamic force feedback deliver satisfying responsiveness. Designed for comfort, control, and productivity, it’s built to keep up.
Navigate with Effortless Precision
Get precise, quiet navigation with a durable touchpad built to last. Whisper-quiet with every swipe and tap, it’s designed for comfort and control, making it ideal for extended work sessions or creative projects without unnecessary distractions.
Hear More and Feel More
Feel every beat, word, and note over four powerful speakers, certified by Dolby Atmos®. Whether you’re streaming or jamming, the upgraded woofer yields clarity and stunning bass sound that bring each moment to life in incredible depth and detail.
Clear Voice, Crisp Vision
Capture each word clearly with four noise-canceling 3D array mics and 360° spatial audio that picks up voices from all directions. Built-in Voice ID isolates your voice while the 5M IR camera delivers detailed visuals for a professional experience.
LENOVO AI APPS
Smarter, Faster, and Safer
Get more done with Lenovo's AI-powered apps, designed to adapt to your needs. These apps go beyond just simplifying tasks — they personalize your experience, boost productivity, and protect your data. Whether it’s big projects or everyday tasks, Lenovo AI Apps deliver evolving performance with limitless potential to create and achieve more.
YOUR CREATIVE TOOLKIT
Professional Creative Tools, on Us
Your laptop includes a free 2-month membership to Adobe Creative Cloud*. Start a new membership of the entire suite with no payment or credit card information required at time of redemption. Already a member? No problem. Your existing payment method will be paused for two months. (Over $100 added value with no cost to you.) Terms apply. Click here for details!

*Available via Lenovo Vantage
YOGA ACCESSORIES
Seamless Sound and Control
Complete your setup with Yoga Pro 7i Aura Edition’s optional connected gear. The Yoga 14(35.56 cms) Sleeve keeps your PC protected, while the Lenovo TWS Earbuds Yoga PC Edition deliver crystal-clear sound and Active Noise Cancellation (ANC) for immersive audio. The Pro Mouse provides smooth, wireless navigation for your everyday use.

*Wireless mouse and earbuds shown with laptop sold separately.
A PC BUILT RESPONSIBLY
Sustainability
A step towards a finer planet, the Carbon Neutral Certified*, ENERGY STAR®-rated, and EPEAT® Gold-registered** Yoga Pro 7i Aura Edition achieves plastic-free packaging. All paper boxes used in packaging are FSC™-certified and made from other controlled material.*** It's built with 50% recycled aluminum in the bottom cover. 

*Based on reduction efforts and carbon offset purchases. Learn more about the carbon-neutral reports at https://www.lenovo.com/in/en/carbonneutral. Carbon neutrality certification was issued by TÜV Rheinland Greater China in accordance with PAS 2060:2014 Specification for the Demonstration of Carbon Neutrality. Learn more about our carbon-neutral reports at https://www.lenovo.com/in/en/carbonneutral
**EPEAT-registered where applicable -- see www.epeat.net for registration status by country.
***FSC License codes: C170715 with 50% recycled aluminum in the bottom cover.

Extremely Disappointed – Bluetooth Mic Doesnt Work
Kothuru Manoj Kumar
VERIFIED PURCHASER
5 months ago
Bought the Lenovo Yoga 7i Aura Edition expecting a premium device, but it fails at the basics. The Bluetooth headset mic doesn’t work in any apps — only in Windows test mode. It’s like buying a luxury car that can’t honk. Disabling Dolby Atmos temporarily fixes it, proving it’s a software flaw. Lenovo support couldn’t resolve it even after sending a technician. Not recommended until they fix this issue.

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now

4 out of 5 stars.
A Everyday Laptop with Premium Build and Display
Akash_K
VERIFIED PURCHASER
8 months ago
The laptop is overall very good. Its standout feature is the display — sharp, bright, and excellent in quality, though it tends to pick up fingerprints easily. The touchscreen works smoothly, and the keyboard is one of the best I’ve used so far. The trackpad, however, could have been better. In terms of performance, it handles my everyday tasks well, including heavy browser use, AI tools, and Microsoft Office. The battery backup is decent — not exceptional but reliable enough for regular work. The charger adapter gets slightly warm during use, but nothing concerning. The body material feels premium, being fully metal, yet it is light and very easy to carry.

OUR PROMISE TO YOU
Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.
Learn More >

PURESIGHT PRO
Precision in Every Pixel
Precise visuals pop on a 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with perfect color accuracy, 120Hz refresh rate, and HDR brilliance. A 90.8% screen-to-body ratio expands your view, while TÜV low blue light tech reduces eye strain for marathon sessions.
MORE PRODUCTIVE AND CREATIVE
It's Possible on Your Intel® AI PC
Work, create, innovate, and experience the best AI PC performance with Intel® Core™ Ultra processors. AI acceleration via a 72 TOPS iGPU optimizes workflows, speeding up creative tasks like animation, 3D rendering, and video editing. The ultimate performance lets you do more with ease, without sacrificing peace of mind. 
LENOVO X POWER
Create at the Speed of X
The overclocked RAM helps push performance to new levels, valuable for high-bandwidth tasks like video editing or data processing. AIDA64 memory benchmark testing shows significant improvements, including faster data transfer and reduced latency.
WELCOME TO LENOVO AURA EDITION
Signature Imagination with Intel®
Lenovo and Intel® have long joined forces to engineer the best laptops in the industry. Our years of deep collaboration now culminate in bold new software solutions that elevate your day-to-day experience. The best products. The best experiences. Lenovo Aura Edition.
MULTIDEVICE SYNC
Just Tap to Connect
Smart Share connects your smartphone to your laptop instantly via an AI virtual sensor. Just tap your Android™ or iOS device on your laptop — then drag and drop. Edit photos and share easily. Plus, access and send text messages from your PC.*

*To use the tap-and-share feature, the Smart Share app must be running.
EXPERIENCE THE INTELLIGENCE OF AURA
Smart Modes, Smarter Technology
*Selected models may require a software update to access all features shown in the images and videos.
Collaboration Mode
Improve your virtual meeting experiences. Keep the focus on you with background blur, low-light enhancer, autoframing, and a virtual presenter. Preview video before joining a call. Expect more engaging communication that puts you in control.
Attention Mode
Minimize distractions so you can focus. You choose the domains and apps you want to block for a set amount of time to keep you immersed in the task at hand.
Power Mode
Reduce power consumption and boost performance when unplugged. Power Mode optimizes settings and finds the ideal balance between improved battery life and better battery performance.
Wellness Mode
Promote digital well-being to keep your health at the forefront. Alerts encourage breaks for your eyes, with clear guidance to shift your sight to something in the distance. Plus, relying on Al sensors, reminders foster good ergonomic habits.
Shield Mode
Proactively enhance data security and privacy. This mode prompts for your preferred VPN when connecting to WiFi, notifies you if someone looks over your shoulder, and blurs your screen to guard privacy if someone is detected near your device.

PREMIUM SUITE
Work Smarter, Achieve More

The silent touchpad glides effortlessly, and Dolby Atmos® sound with four speakers that achieve 80.5db volume and 126Hz low-frequency bass, providing immersive sound. Enjoy clear visuals and noise-canceling mics for every call and project.
The Bliss is in the Details
Precision in Every Keystroke
The Yoga-coated keyboard resists oil and water for a clean, premium feel, while 1.5mm key travel, 0.3mm dish caps, and dynamic force feedback deliver satisfying responsiveness. Designed for comfort, control, and productivity, it’s built to keep up.
Navigate with Effortless Precision
Get precise, quiet navigation with a durable touchpad built to last. Whisper-quiet with every swipe and tap, it’s designed for comfort and control, making it ideal for extended work sessions or creative projects without unnecessary distractions.
Hear More and Feel More
Feel every beat, word, and note over four powerful speakers, certified by Dolby Atmos®. Whether you’re streaming or jamming, the upgraded woofer yields clarity and stunning bass sound that bring each moment to life in incredible depth and detail.
Clear Voice, Crisp Vision
Capture each word clearly with four noise-canceling 3D array mics and 360° spatial audio that picks up voices from all directions. Built-in Voice ID isolates your voice while the 5M IR camera delivers detailed visuals for a professional experience.

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now
What is the Primary Use of this Product?School
Yes, I recommend this product.

Build & Design: The laptop has a stunning, premium design with a sleek aluminum chassis. The 14.5" 3K PureSight display is gorgeous, with vibrant colors, high brightness, and super-smooth 120Hz refresh rate. Ideal for both work and content consumption. Final Verdict: The Lenovo Yoga Pro 7i Gen 10 Aura Edition is one of the best laptops in its class — blending power, portability, and aesthetics beautifully. Whether you're a student, content creator, or professional, this laptop won’t disappoint. Highly recommended! 💻🔥

OUR PROMISE TO YOU
Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.

PURESIGHT PRO
Precision in Every Pixel
Precise visuals pop on a 14.5(36.83 cms) 3K OLED PureSight Pro display with perfect color accuracy, 120Hz refresh rate, and HDR brilliance. A 90.8% screen-to-body ratio expands your view, while TÜV low blue light tech reduces eye strain for marathon sessions.
MORE PRODUCTIVE AND CREATIVE
It's Possible on Your Intel® AI PC
Work, create, innovate, and experience the best AI PC performance with Intel® Core™ Ultra processors. AI acceleration via a 72 TOPS iGPU optimizes workflows, speeding up creative tasks like animation, 3D rendering, and video editing. The ultimate performance lets you do more with ease, without sacrificing peace of mind. 
LENOVO X POWER
Create at the Speed of X
The overclocked RAM helps push performance to new levels, valuable for high-bandwidth tasks like video editing or data processing. AIDA64 memory benchmark testing shows significant improvements, including faster data transfer and reduced latency.
WELCOME TO LENOVO AURA EDITION
Signature Imagination with Intel®
Lenovo and Intel® have long joined forces to engineer the best laptops in the industry. Our years of deep collaboration now culminate in bold new software solutions that elevate your day-to-day experience. The best products. The best experiences. Lenovo Aura Edition.
MULTIDEVICE SYNC
Just Tap to Connect
Smart Share connects your smartphone to your laptop instantly via an AI virtual sensor. Just tap your Android™ or iOS device on your laptop — then drag and drop. Edit photos and share easily. Plus, access and send text messages from your PC.*

*To use the tap-and-share feature, the Smart Share app must be running.
EXPERIENCE THE INTELLIGENCE OF AURA
Smart Modes, Smarter Technology
*Selected models may require a software update to access all features shown in the images and videos.
Collaboration Mode
Improve your virtual meeting experiences. Keep the focus on you with background blur, low-light enhancer, autoframing, and a virtual presenter. Preview video before joining a call. Expect more engaging communication that puts you in control.
Attention Mode
Minimize distractions so you can focus. You choose the domains and apps you want to block for a set amount of time to keep you immersed in the task at hand.
Power Mode
Reduce power consumption and boost performance when unplugged. Power Mode optimizes settings and finds the ideal balance between improved battery life and better battery performance.
Wellness Mode
Promote digital well-being to keep your health at the forefront. Alerts encourage breaks for your eyes, with clear guidance to shift your sight to something in the distance. Plus, relying on Al sensors, reminders foster good ergonomic habits.
Shield Mode
Proactively enhance data security and privacy. This mode prompts for your preferred VPN when connecting to WiFi, notifies you if someone looks over your shoulder, and blurs your screen to guard privacy if someone is detected near your device.

The Yoga-coated keyboard resists oil and water for a clean, premium feel, while 1.5mm key travel, 0.3mm dish caps, and dynamic force feedback deliver satisfying responsiveness. Designed for comfort, control, and productivity, it’s built to keep up.

Clear Voice, Crisp Vision

5 out of 5 stars.
Overview
Derick
VERIFIED PURCHASER
2 months ago
The Visual & Auditory Experience The standout feature is, without a doubt, the OLED display. It is absolutely stunning—blacks are perfectly deep, and the colors pop with a level of vibrancy that makes standard IPS screens look dull. Whether you're color-grading a project or just watching a movie, the contrast is breathtaking. Equally surprising are the speakers. Laptop audio is usually an afterthought, but these are easily the best speakers I’ve ever heard on a portable machine. The soundstage is wide, and there’s a genuine richness to the audio that fills a room, making external speakers almost unnecessary for casual use. Built for Productivity • Keyboard & Trackpad: The typing experience is classic Lenovo—tactile, snappy, and deeply satisfying for long writing sessions. This is paired with an impressively large trackpad that feels smooth and responsive, offering plenty of real estate for multi-touch gestures. • Port Selection: Unlike the "dongle life" required by many modern machines, this laptop has plenty of ports. You won’t find yourself hunting for an adapter just to plug in a USB drive or an external monitor. • Form Factor: While it isn't "razor-thin," it remains remarkably lightweight. It feels substantial enough to be durable but is easy to toss into a backpack without straining your shoulder—a great balance for those who travel frequently. Performance: Gaming & AI Don’t let the professional look fool you; this machine has serious power. I tested it with Forza Horizon 5 and the new FC26, and it handled both with ease. The frame rates remained stable, and the gameplay was fluid even at Medium settings. The Lenovo AI features also deserve a mention. It’s not just a gimmick—it’s actually useful. It intelligently manages thermal profiles and battery life based on what you’re doing, ensuring that when you're gaming, you get the performance you need, and when you're working, the fans stay whisper-quiet. The One Missing Piece If there is one gripe, it’s the omission of a fingerprint sensor. In a world where biometric login is the standard, having to type in a PIN or password feels like a small step backward. I would have loved to see a sensor integrated into the power button for that extra bit of convenience. Final Verdict This is a powerhouse disguised as a sophisticated daily driver. Despite the lack of a fingerprint reader, its combination of a world-class OLED screen, elite speakers, and surprisingly robust gaming performance makes it one of the most versatile laptops on the market right now
What is the Primary Use of this Product?School
Yes, I recommend this product.

Lenovo Services
Premium Care
Advanced support from real people. Real fast. Premium Care is the hassle-free solution for all your technical support needs. Upgrade your standard warranty with our front-of-the-queue customer support service to get the most out of your new device.
Learn More >
Accidental Damage Protection
Life happens! Laptops drop, coffee spills, power surges. With Accidental Damage Protection (ADP) you won’t need to bat an eye. This fixed-cost, fixed-term, protection plan minimizes the cost of unexpected repairs. But perhaps more importantly, it reassures you that we’ve got your back when you need it most.
CO2 Offset Service
The CO2 Offset service is contributing based on the average cost of the carbon emissions associated with selected devices, from manufacturing to shipment and the average lifecycle. We then work with several projects, including those vetted by the United Nations for climate change, so you can trust the impact and integrity of the environmental projects you support. These include improving renewable energy, reducing air pollution, and enhancing safe-waste disposal.

PURESIGHT PRO
Precision in Every Pixel
